PROBLEM
------------------------------
I am practicing the Tower of Hanoi puzzle. Here is the action I can do

Move the top disk from one peg to another peg

I must obey the following rules:
I can move only one disk at a time.
I may only move a disk that is on top of a peg.
I can never place a larger disk on top of a smaller disk.
Once a disk is moved, it keeps its relative size ordering with the others.

[STATEMENT]
There are 7 disks in total. From smallest to largest they are disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G.
As initial conditions I have that, the right peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, while the left peg and the middle peg are empty.
My goal is to have that the middle peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, and both the right peg and the left peg are empty again.
The left peg can be used as an intermediate parking spot but must end up empty.

I will not ask the user for further clarifications and I will report the plan that explicitly states all the (2^7 - 1) intermediate steps to achieve the objective in an optimal way. My plan is as follows:

[PLAN]
================================================================================


ENVIRONMENT
------------------------------
I am practicing the Tower of Hanoi puzzle. Here is the action I can do

Move the top disk from one peg to another peg

I must obey the following rules:
I can move only one disk at a time.
I may only move a disk that is on top of a peg.
I can never place a larger disk on top of a smaller disk.
Once a disk is moved, it keeps its relative size ordering with the others.

[STATEMENT]
There are 7 disks in total. From smallest to largest they are disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G.
As initial conditions I have that, the right peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, while the left peg and the middle peg are empty.
My goal is to have that the middle peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, and both the right peg and the left peg are empty again.
The left peg can be used as an intermediate parking spot but must end up empty.

I will not ask the user for further clarifications and I will report the plan that explicitly states all the (2^7 - 1) intermediate steps to achieve the objective in an optimal way. My plan is as follows:

[PLAN]
================================================================================


DOMAIN
------------------------------
(define (domain hanoi-orchestration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types disk peg slot step agent)

  (:predicates
    ;; physical state
    (at ?d - disk ?p - peg ?s - slot)
    (occupied ?p - peg ?s - slot)

    ;; sequencing and traceability
    (ready ?st - step)
    (step-unmoved ?st - step)
    (moved ?st - step ?d - disk ?fromp - peg ?froms - slot ?top - peg ?tos - slot ?m - agent)
    (verified-step ?st - step)
    (verified-by ?st - step ?a - agent)
    (observed-initial ?a - agent)

    ;; step ordering
    (succ ?s1 - step ?s2 - step)

    ;; disk size relation
    (larger ?big - disk ?small - disk)
  )

  ;; Observer reports initial state (traceable).
  (:action observer-report
    :parameters (?obs - agent)
    :precondition ()
    :effect (observed-initial ?obs)
  )

  ;; Auditor verifies a move and advances the ready step pointer.
  (:action auditor-verify-advance
    :parameters (?st - step ?stn - step ?d - disk ?fp - peg ?fs - slot ?tp - peg ?ts - slot ?aud - agent)
    :precondition (and
      (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud)
      (succ ?st ?stn)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud))
      (verified-step ?st)
      (verified-by ?st ?aud)
      (not (ready ?st))
      (ready ?stn)
    )
  )

  ;; For completeness, allow auditor to finalize the sequence by verifying the last move
  ;; (last step has a successor in the problem as the final readiness marker).
  (:action auditor-verify-final
    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?fp - peg ?fs - slot ?tp - peg ?ts - slot ?aud - agent)
    :precondition (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud)
    :effect (and
      (not (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud))
      (verified-step ?st)
      (verified-by ?st ?aud)
      (not (ready ?st))
    )
  )

  ;; Mover actions: concrete actions for each combination of source slot and target slot.
  ;; We provide a fully expanded set of move templates; each is guarded to ensure:
  ;; - the moved disk is present at the stated source slot,
  ;; - all slots above the source slot on that peg are empty (so the disk is the top disk on its peg),
  ;; - the target slot is the immediate top slot on the target peg (so the disk ends up on top),
  ;; - if placing onto an existing disk (target slot > 1) the disk below is larger than the moving disk,
  ;; - the step is the current ready step, the step has not yet had a move (step-unmoved),
  ;; - the observer has already reported the initial state (observed-initial).
  ;;
  ;; There are 7 source-slot x 7 target-slot templates; each template is generic in pegs and disks.
  ;; Each template name encodes the numeric slots moved-from and moved-to.
  ;; For space and clarity we enumerate them explicitly.

  ;; Helper note: slot names are slot1 (bottom) .. slot7 (top).
  ;; Precondition patterns below reference specific slot constants and explicit "not (occupied ...)" checks
  ;; to enforce "topness" constraints without arithmetic operations.

  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot1
  (:action move-slot1-to-slot1
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st)
      (step-unmoved ?st)
      (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot1)
      ;; ensure disk is top on source: no occupied slots above slot1
      (not (occupied ?from slot2)) (not (occupied ?from slot3))
      (not (occupied ?from slot4)) (not (occupied ?from slot5))
      (not (occupied ?from slot6)) (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      ;; target slot1 must be the immediate top slot on target peg:
      (not (occupied ?to slot1))
      (not (occupied ?to slot2)) (not (occupied ?to slot3))
      (not (occupied ?to slot4)) (not (occupied ?to slot5))
      (not (occupied ?to slot6)) (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      ;; placing at bottom slot => no below-disk size check
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot1))
      (at ?d ?to slot1)
      (not (occupied ?from slot1))
      (occupied ?to slot1)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot1 ?to slot1 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot2
  (:action move-slot1-to-slot2
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st)
      (step-unmoved ?st)
      (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot1)
      ;; source topness
      (not (occupied ?from slot2)) (not (occupied ?from slot3))
      (not (occupied ?from slot4)) (not (occupied ?from slot5))
      (not (occupied ?from slot6)) (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      ;; target immediate top at slot2:
      (not (occupied ?to slot2))
      (not (occupied ?to slot3)) (not (occupied ?to slot4))
      (not (occupied ?to slot5)) (not (occupied ?to slot6))
      (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      ;; slot1 (below) must be occupied and that disk must be larger than the moving disk
      (occupied ?to slot1)
      (at ?below ?to slot1)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot1))
      (at ?d ?to slot2)
      (not (occupied ?from slot1))
      (occupied ?to slot2)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot1 ?to slot2 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot3
  (:action move-slot1-to-slot3
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot1)
      ;; source top
      (not (occupied ?from slot2)) (not (occupied ?from slot3))
      (not (occupied ?from slot4)) (not (occupied ?from slot5))
      (not (occupied ?from slot6)) (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      ;; target slot3 must be immediate top (slot2 below must be occupied)
      (not (occupied ?to slot3))
      (not (occupied ?to slot4)) (not (occupied ?to slot5))
      (not (occupied ?to slot6)) (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot2)
      (at ?below ?to slot2)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot1))
      (at ?d ?to slot3)
      (not (occupied ?from slot1))
      (occupied ?to slot3)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot1 ?to slot3 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot4
  (:action move-slot1-to-slot4
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and

  )

      ;; source top
      (not (occupied ?from slot2)) (not (occupied ?from slot3))

      (not (occupied ?from slot6)) (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      ;; target immediate top at slot5:
      (not (occupied ?to slot5))
      (not (occupied ?to slot6)) (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot4)
      (at ?below ?to slot4)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot1))
      (at ?d ?to slot5)
      (not (occupied ?from slot1))
      (occupied ?to slot5)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot1 ?to slot5 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot6
  (:action move-slot1-to-slot6
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)

      ;; source top
      (not (occupied ?from slot2)) (not (occupied ?from slot3))

      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot3)
      (not (occupied ?from slot4)) (not (occupied ?from slot5))
      (not (occupied ?from slot6)) (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      (not (occupied ?to slot5))
      (not (occupied ?to slot6)) (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot4)
      (at ?below ?to slot4)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot3))
      (at ?d ?to slot5)
      (not (occupied ?from slot3))
      (occupied ?to slot5)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot3 ?to slot5 ?m)
    )
  )

      (occupied ?to slot2)
      (at ?below ?to slot2)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot7))
      (at ?d ?to slot3)
      (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot3)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot7 ?to slot3 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot7 -> slot4
  (:action move-slot7-to-slot4
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot7)
      (not (occupied ?to slot4))
      (not (occupied ?to slot5)) (not (occupied ?to slot6))
      (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot3)
      (at ?below ?to slot3)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot7))
      (at ?d ?to slot4)
      (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot4)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot7 ?to slot4 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot7 -> slot5
  (:action move-slot7-to-slot5
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot7)
      (not (occupied ?to slot5))
      (not (occupied ?to slot6)) (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot4)
      (at ?below ?to slot4)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot7))
      (at ?d ?to slot5)
      (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot5)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot7 ?to slot5 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot7 -> slot6
  (:action move-slot7-to-slot6
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot7)
      (not (occupied ?to slot6))
      (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot5)
      (at ?below ?to slot5)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot7))
      (at ?d ?to slot6)
      (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot6)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot7 ?to slot6 ?m)
    )
  )

  ;; Move from slot7 -> slot7
  (:action move-slot7-to-slot7
    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)
    :precondition (and
      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)
      (not (= ?from ?to))
      (at ?d ?from slot7)
      (not (occupied ?to slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot6)
      (at ?below ?to slot6)
      (larger ?below ?d)
    )
    :effect (and
      (not (at ?d ?from slot7))
      (at ?d ?to slot7)
      (not (occupied ?from slot7))
      (occupied ?to slot7)
      (not (step-unmoved ?st))
      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot7 ?to slot7 ?m)
    )
  )

(define (problem hanoi-7-orchestration-problem)
  (:domain hanoi-orchestration)
  (:objects
    ;; disks: d1 smallest ... d7 largest
    d1 d2 d3 d4 d5 d6 d7 - disk

sequencing and traceability\n    (ready ?st - step)\n    (step-unmoved ?st - step)\n    (moved ?st - step ?d - disk ?fromp - peg ?froms - slot ?top - peg ?tos - slot ?m - agent)\n    (verified-step ?st - step)\n    (verified-by ?st - step ?a - agent)\n    (observed-initial ?a - agent)\n\n    ;; step ordering\n    (succ ?s1 - step ?s2 - step)\n\n    ;; disk size relation\n    (larger ?big - disk ?small - disk)\n  )\n\n  ;; Observer reports initial state (traceable).\n  (:action observer-report\n    :parameters (?obs - agent)\n    :precondition ()\n    :effect (observed-initial ?obs)\n  )\n\n  ;; Auditor verifies a move and advances the ready step pointer.\n  (:action auditor-verify-advance\n    :parameters (?st - step ?stn - step ?d - disk ?fp - peg ?fs - slot ?tp - peg ?ts - slot ?aud - agent)\n    :precondition (and\n      (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud)\n      (succ ?st ?stn)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      (not (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (verified-by ?st ?aud)\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (ready ?stn)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; For completeness, allow auditor to finalize the sequence by verifying the last move\n  ;; (last step has a successor in the problem as the final readiness marker).\n  (:action auditor-verify-final\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?fp - peg ?fs - slot ?tp - peg ?ts - slot ?aud - agent)\n    :precondition (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud)\n    :effect (and\n      (not (moved ?st ?d ?fp ?fs ?tp ?ts ?aud))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (verified-by ?st ?aud)\n      (not (ready ?st))\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Mover actions: concrete actions for each combination of source slot and target slot.\n  ;; We provide a fully expanded set of move templates; each is guarded to ensure:\n  ;; - the moved disk is present at the stated source slot,\n  ;; - all slots above the source slot on that peg are empty (so the disk is the top disk on its peg),\n  ;; - the target slot is the immediate top slot on the target peg (so the disk ends up on top),\n  ;; - if placing onto an existing disk (target slot > 1) the disk below is larger than the moving disk,\n  ;; - the step is the current ready step, the step has not yet had a move (step-unmoved),\n  ;; - the observer has already reported the initial state (observed-initial).\n  ;;\n  ;; There are 7 source-slot x 7 target-slot templates; each template is generic in pegs and disks.\n  ;; Each template name encodes the numeric slots moved-from and moved-to.\n  ;; For space and clarity we enumerate them explicitly.\n\n  ;; Helper note: slot names are slot1 (bottom) .. slot7 (top).\n  ;; Precondition patterns below reference specific slot constants and explicit \"not (occupied ...)\" checks\n  ;; to enforce \"topness\" constraints without arithmetic operations.\n\n  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot1\n  (:action move-slot1-to-slot1\n    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (observed-initial ?m)\n      (not (= ?from ?to))\n      (at ?d ?from slot1)\n      ;; ensure disk is top on source: no occupied slots above slot1\n      (not (occupied ?from slot2)) (not (occupied ?from slot3))\n      (not (occupied ?from slot4)) (not (occupied ?from slot5))\n      (not (occupied ?from slot6)) (not (occupied ?from slot7))\n      ;; target slot1 must be the immediate top slot on target peg:\n      (not (occupied ?to slot1))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot2)) (not (occupied ?to slot3))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot4)) (not (occupied ?to slot5))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot6)) (not (occupied ?to slot7))\n      ;; placing at bottom slot => no below-disk size check\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      (not (at ?d ?from slot1))\n      (at ?d ?to slot1)\n      (not (occupied ?from slot1))\n      (occupied ?to slot1)\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot1 ?to slot1 ?m)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot2\n  (:action move-slot1-to-slot2\n    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (observed-initial ?m)\n      (not (= ?from ?to))\n      (at ?d ?from slot1)\n      ;; source topness\n      (not (occupied ?from slot2)) (not (occupied ?from slot3))\n      (not (occupied ?from slot4)) (not (occupied ?from slot5))\n      (not (occupied ?from slot6)) (not (occupied ?from slot7))\n      ;; target immediate top at slot2:\n      (not (occupied ?to slot2))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot3)) (not (occupied ?to slot4))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot5)) (not (occupied ?to slot6))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot7))\n      ;; slot1 (below) must be occupied and that disk must be larger than the moving disk\n      (occupied ?to slot1)\n      (at ?below ?to slot1)\n      (larger ?below ?d)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      (not (at ?d ?from slot1))\n      (at ?d ?to slot2)\n      (not (occupied ?from slot1))\n      (occupied ?to slot2)\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot1 ?to slot2 ?m)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move from slot1 -> slot3\n  (:action move-slot1-to-slot3\n    :parameters (?st - step ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?below - disk)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st) (step-unmoved ?st) (observed-initial ?m)\n      (not (= ?from ?to))\n      (at ?d ?from slot1)\n      ;; target slot3 must be immediate top (slot2 below must be occupied)\n      (not (occupied ?to slot3))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot4)) (not (occupied ?to slot5))\n      (not (occupied ?to slot6)) (not (occupied ?to slot7))\n      (occupied ?to slot2)\n      (at ?below ?to slot2)\n      (larger ?below ?d)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      (not (at ?d ?from slot1))\n      (at ?d ?to slot3)\n      (not (occupied ?from slot1))\n      (occupied ?to slot3)\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (moved ?st ?d ?from slot1 ?to slot3 ?m)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; disk is directly on a place (peg or another disk)\n    (clear ?p - place)               ;; nothing is directly on top of this place (peg or disk)\n    (larger ?big - disk ?small - disk)\n\n    (ready ?s - step)\n    (step-unmoved ?s - step)\n    (moved ?s - step ?d - disk ?from - place ?to - place ?m - agent)\n\n    (succ ?s1 - step ?s2 - step)\n    (verified-step ?s - step)\n    (verified-by ?s - step ?a - agent)\n\n    (observed-initial ?a - agent)\n  )\n\n  ;; Observer must record initial observation before moves are allowed to use it.\n  (:action observer-report\n    :parameters (?obs - agent)\n    :precondition (and)\n    :effect (and\n      (observed-initial ?obs)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move a top disk onto an empty place (peg or an empty place).\n  (:action move-to-empty\n    :parameters (?st - step ?obs - agent ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - place ?to - place)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (observed-initial ?obs)\n      (on ?d ?from)\n      (clear ?d)         ;; disk must be top on its source place\n      (clear ?to)        ;; target place must be clear (no disk directly on it)\n      ;; disallow placing a disk onto itself\n      (not (= ?from ?to))\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; relocate disk\n      (not (on ?d ?from))\n      (on ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; source place becomes clear after removing its top disk\n      (clear ?from)\n      ;; target place is no longer clear (now has disk on top)\n      (not (clear ?to))\n\n      ;; bookkeeping for the step\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (moved ?st ?d ?from ?to ?m)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move a top disk onto another disk (target must be a disk and larger).\n  (:action move-onto-disk\n    :parameters (?st - step ?obs - agent ?m - agent ?d - disk ?from - place ?to - disk ?to_on - place)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (observed-initial ?obs)\n      (on ?d ?from)\n      (clear ?d)\n      (on ?to ?to_on)    ;; the target disk must currently be on some place\n      (clear ?to)        ;; the target disk must be top on its place\n      (larger ?to ?d)    ;; size constraint: target disk is larger than moving disk\n      ;; disallow trivial self-move\n      (not (= ?d ?to))\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      (not (on ?d ?from))\n      (on ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; source becomes clear after removal\n      (clear ?from)\n      ;; target disk is no longer clear\n      (not (clear ?to))\n\n      ;; step bookkeeping\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (moved ?st ?d ?from ?to ?m)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Auditor verifies the recorded moved step and enables the successor step.\n  (:action auditor-verify-advance\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?from - place ?to - place ?m - agent ?aud - agent ?stn - step)\n    :precondition (and\n      (moved ?st ?d ?from ?to ?m)\n      (succ ?st ?stn)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      (not (moved ?st ?d ?from ?to ?m))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (verified-by ?st ?aud)\n      (ready ?stn)\n    )\n  )\n)",

disk has no disk directly on top (is top of its stack)\n\n    ;; size ordering\n    (smaller ?d1 - disk ?d2 - disk)  ;; ?d1 is smaller than ?d2\n\n    ;; step sequencing and verification\n    (ready ?st - step)\n    (step-unmoved ?st - step)\n    (verified-step ?st - step)\n    (succ ?s1 - step ?s2 - step)\n  )\n\n  ;; Move a disk that is directly on a peg to an empty peg\n  (:action move-peg-to-peg\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?next - step)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (on-peg ?d ?from)\n      (clear-disk ?d)\n      (clear-peg ?to)\n      (succ ?st ?next)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; update stacking\n      (not (on-peg ?d ?from))\n      (on-peg ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; pegs become empty/non-empty accordingly\n      (clear-peg ?from)\n      (not (clear-peg ?to))\n\n      ;; step sequencing bookkeeping (enforce one move per step)\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (ready ?next)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move a disk that is directly on a peg onto another disk (destination must be larger)\n  (:action move-peg-to-disk\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - disk ?next - step)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (on-peg ?d ?from)\n      (clear-disk ?d)\n      (clear-disk ?to)\n      (smaller ?d ?to)\n      (succ ?st ?next)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; update stacking\n      (not (on-peg ?d ?from))\n      (on-disk ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; peg becomes empty\n      (clear-peg ?from)\n\n      ;; destination disk no longer clear (has disk on top)\n      (not (clear-disk ?to))\n\n      ;; step sequencing bookkeeping\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (ready ?next)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move a disk that is directly on another disk onto an empty peg\n  (:action move-disk-to-peg\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?from - disk ?to - peg ?next - step)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (on-disk ?d ?from)\n      (clear-disk ?d)\n      (clear-peg ?to)\n      (succ ?st ?next)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; update stacking\n      (not (on-disk ?d ?from))\n      (on-peg ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; the disk that supported ?d is now clear (no disk on it)\n      (clear-disk ?from)\n\n      ;; destination peg becomes non-empty\n      (not (clear-peg ?to))\n\n      ;; step sequencing bookkeeping\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (ready ?next)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move a disk that is directly on another disk onto another disk (destination must be larger)\n  (:action move-disk-to-disk\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?from - disk ?to - disk ?next - step)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (on-disk ?d ?from)\n      (clear-disk ?d)\n      (clear-disk ?to)\n      (smaller ?d ?to)\n      (succ ?st ?next)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; update stacking\n      (not (on-disk ?d ?from))\n      (on-disk ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; the disk that supported ?d is now clear\n      (clear-disk ?from)\n\n      ;; destination disk no longer clear\n      (not (clear-disk ?to))\n\n      ;; step sequencing bookkeeping\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (ready ?next)\n    )\n  )\n)",

    "pddl_domain": "(define (domain hanoi)\n  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)\n  (:types disk peg step)\n\n  (:predicates\n    ;; placement relations: disk is directly on a peg or on another disk\n    (on-peg ?d - disk ?p - peg)\n    (on-disk ?d - disk ?s - disk)\n\n    ;; clear means nothing sits on that peg or disk (i.e., it is available as a destination or movable)\n    (clear-peg ?p - peg)\n    (clear-disk ?d - disk)\n\n    ;; size ordering between disks\n    (smaller ?d1 - disk ?d2 - disk)\n\n    ;; step control / sequencing\n    (ready ?st - step)\n    (step-unmoved ?st - step)\n    (verified-step ?st - step)\n    (succ ?s1 - step ?s2 - step)\n  )\n\n  ;; Move top disk that is directly on a peg to an empty peg\n  (:action move-peg-to-peg\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - peg ?next - step)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (on-peg ?d ?from)\n      (clear-disk ?d)\n      (clear-peg ?to)\n      (succ ?st ?next)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; update placement\n      (not (on-peg ?d ?from))\n      (on-peg ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; source peg becomes clear (disk was directly on that peg)\n      (clear-peg ?from)\n      ;; destination peg now occupied on top\n      (not (clear-peg ?to))\n\n      ;; step bookkeeping\n      (not (step-unmoved ?st))\n      (not (ready ?st))\n      (verified-step ?st)\n      (ready ?next)\n    )\n  )\n\n  ;; Move top disk that is directly on a peg to sit on top of another disk\n  (:action move-peg-to-disk\n    :parameters (?st - step ?d - disk ?from - peg ?to - disk ?next - step)\n    :precondition (and\n      (ready ?st)\n      (step-unmoved ?st)\n      (on-peg ?d ?from)\n      (clear-disk ?d)\n      (clear-disk ?to)\n      (smaller ?d ?to)\n      (succ ?st ?next)\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; update placement\n      (not (on-peg ?d ?from))\n      (on-disk ?d ?to)\n\n      ;; source peg becomes clear\n      (clear-peg ?from)\n      ;; destination disk no longer clear (has d on it)\n      (not (clear-disk ?to))\n\n      ;; PROBLEM
------------------------------
I am practicing the Tower of Hanoi puzzle. Here is the action I can do

Move the top disk from one peg to another peg

I must obey the following rules:
I can move only one disk at a time.
I may only move a disk that is on top of a peg.
I can never place a larger disk on top of a smaller disk.
Once a disk is moved, it keeps its relative size ordering with the others.

[STATEMENT]
There are 7 disks in total. From smallest to largest they are disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G.
As initial conditions I have that, the right peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, while the middle peg and the left peg are empty.
My goal is to have that the left peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, and both the right peg and the middle peg are empty again.
The middle peg can be used as an intermediate parking spot but must end up empty.

I will not ask the user for further clarifications and I will report the plan that explicitly states all the (2^7 - 1) intermediate steps to achieve the objective in an optimal way. My plan is as follows:

[PLAN]
================================================================================


ENVIRONMENT
------------------------------
I am practicing the Tower of Hanoi puzzle. Here is the action I can do

Move the top disk from one peg to another peg

I must obey the following rules:
I can move only one disk at a time.
I may only move a disk that is on top of a peg.
I can never place a larger disk on top of a smaller disk.
Once a disk is moved, it keeps its relative size ordering with the others.

[STATEMENT]
There are 7 disks in total. From smallest to largest they are disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G.
As initial conditions I have that, the right peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, while the middle peg and the left peg are empty.
My goal is to have that the left peg holds, from top to bottom, disk A, disk B, disk C, disk D, disk E, disk F, and disk G, and both the right peg and the middle peg are empty again.
The middle peg can be used as an intermediate parking spot but must end up empty.

I will not ask the user for further clarifications and I will report the plan that explicitly states all the (2^7 - 1) intermediate steps to achieve the objective in an optimal way. My plan is as follows:

DOMAIN
------------------------------
(define (domain hanoi-multiagent)
  ;; Tower of Hanoi domain for FastDownward-compatible STRIPS planning
  ;; Types:
  ;;  - place: an abstract type for supports (pegs and disks)
  ;;  - peg  and disk are subtypes of place
  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)
  (:types place peg disk)

  ;; Predicates:
  ;; (on ?d ?s)         : disk ?d is directly on support ?s (support = peg or disk)
  ;; (onpeg ?d ?p)      : disk ?d is located on base peg ?p (the peg under its stack)
  ;; (clear ?s)         : support ?s (peg or disk) has nothing on top (i.e., it is top)
  ;; (smaller ?d1 ?d2)  : disk ?d1 is strictly smaller than disk ?d2
  ;; The planning instance will provide the concrete initial facts for these predicates.
  (:predicates
    (on ?d - disk ?s - place)
    (onpeg ?d - disk ?p - peg)
    (clear ?s - place)
    (smaller ?d1 - disk ?d2 - disk)
    ;; The next predicates are used if a planner trace-enforcing ordering is required.
    ;; They are included to allow expressing explicit ordered-step constraints in the problem.
    (step-done ?st)
    (step-enabled ?st)
    (planned-move ?st ?d - disk ?src - peg ?dst - peg)
    (next-step ?st1 ?st2)
  )

  ;; Single primitive action: move the top disk associated with a source peg to a destination peg.
  ;; The action is guarded so it can only move a disk when:
  ;;  - the disk is currently the top item of its source peg (onpeg ?d ?src and clear ?d)
  ;;  - the destination peg's top (if any) is larger than the moving disk, or the destination peg is empty (clear ?dst)
  ;; To support both placing onto an empty peg and onto another disk, the action requires the current
  ;; immediate support of the moved disk (?support) and, when placing onto a disk, the target top disk (?target-top).
  ;; Note: We keep one action schema that supports both cases by requiring the caller/environment ensure
  ;; the appropriate clear/size facts for the destination.
  (:action move-top
    :parameters (?st ?next - (either ?step ?step)
                ?d - disk
                ?support - place
                ?src - peg
                ?dst - peg
                ?target-top - disk)
    :precondition (and
      ;; sequencing guard: if the problem includes planned-move facts and step enabling, require step-enabled
      (or (not (planned-move ?st ?d ?src ?dst)) (step-enabled ?st))
      ;; the disk is directly on its immediate support
      (on ?d ?support)
      ;; the disk is reported as associated to source peg
      (onpeg ?d ?src)
      ;; the disk is top of whatever it's on (no disk above)
      (clear ?d)
      ;; destination is either empty (no disk on top of the peg) OR has a top disk ?target-top which is clear and larger
      ;; We express this by requiring either (clear ?dst) or (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (clear ?target-top) (smaller ?d ?target-top))
      ;; Because STRIPS does not have direct OR, callers must ensure one of these holds in the initial state evolution.
      ;; We'll test both forms at runtime through the available predicates.
      ;; For safety we require that either the destination peg is clear OR the indicated top disk exists and is larger.
      ;; (The planner must ensure one of these is true for the action to be applicable.)
      (or (clear ?dst) (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (clear ?target-top) (smaller ?d ?target-top)))
    )
    :effect (and
      ;; sequencing effects: mark this step done and enable successor step if planning a fully-ordered execution
      (when (planned-move ?st ?d ?src ?dst)
        (and (not (step-enabled ?st)) (step-done ?st) (step-enabled ?next)))
      ;; update structural relations for the moved disk: remove its old on fact and set its new direct support
      (not (on ?d ?support))
      ;; When placing on empty peg, direct support becomes the dst peg; when placing on top of another disk, new support becomes that disk.
      ;; Because the action includes ?target-top param, we cover both cases:
      ;; If destination was empty, the new direct support is the destination peg (we add on ?d ?dst).
      ;; If destination had a top disk ?target-top, the new direct support is that disk (we add on ?d ?target-top).
      (or
        (and (clear ?dst) (on ?d ?dst))
        (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (not (clear ?target-top)) (on ?d ?target-top))
      )
      ;; update onpeg (base peg) mapping: the moved disk is now associated with destination peg
      (not (onpeg ?d ?src))
      (onpeg ?d ?dst)
      ;; update clear flags:
      ;; the moved disk remains clear (it is top on its new support)
      ;; the previous support becomes clear (since d was top on it and moved)
      (clear ?support)
      ;; the destination support (peg or disk) is no longer clear after placing d on it
      (not (clear ?dst))
      (when (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (clear ?target-top))
        (not (clear ?target-top)))
    )
  )
)

(define (problem hanoi-7-disks)
  (:domain hanoi-multiagent)

  ;; Objects: 7 disks A..G and three pegs Left, Middle, Right.
  (:objects
    A B C D E F G - disk
    Left Middle Right - peg
    ;; steps are optional scaffolding to express ordered execution if needed by the planner
    s1 s2 s3 s4 s5 s6 s7 s8 s9 s10 s11 s12 s13 s14 s15 s16 s17 s18 s19 s20
    s21 s22 s23 s24 s25 s26 s27 s28 s29 s30 s31 s32 s33 s34 s35 s36 s37 s38 s39 s40
    s41 s42 s43 s44 s45 s46 s47 s48 s49 s50 s51 s52 s53 s54 s55 s56 s57 s58 s59 s60
    s61 s62 s63 s64 s65 s66 s67 s68 s69 s70 s71 s72 s73 s74 s75 s76 s77 s78 s79 s80
    s81 s82 s83 s84 s85 s86 s87 s88 s89 s90 s91 s92 s93 s94 s95 s96 s97 s98 s99 s100
    s101 s102 s103 s104 s105 s106 s107 s108 s109 s110 s111 s112 s113 s114 s115 s116 s117 s118 s119 s120
    s121 s122 s123 s124 s125 s126 s127 s128 - step
  )

  ;; Initial State:
  ;; All disks are stacked on Right (top A ... bottom G).
  ;; We represent direct-on relations (on) with immediate support,
  ;; and onpeg mapping (onpeg) to indicate each disk's base peg (Right).
  (:init
    ;; size ordering (smaller is true for pairs where left is smaller than right)
    (smaller A B) (smaller A C) (smaller A D) (smaller A E) (smaller A F) (smaller A G)
    (smaller B C) (smaller B D) (smaller B E) (smaller B F) (smaller B G)
    (smaller C D) (smaller C E) (smaller C F) (smaller C G)
    (smaller D E) (smaller D F) (smaller D G)
    (smaller E F) (smaller E G)
    (smaller F G)

    ;; direct support chain top->bottom for initial stacking on Right:
    ;; A on B, B on C, ..., F on G, G on Right
    (on A B)
    (on B C)
    (on C D)
    (on D E)
    (on E F)
    (on F G)
    (on G Right)

    ;; base-peg mapping for all disks is Right
    (onpeg A Right)
    (onpeg B Right)
    (onpeg C Right)
    (onpeg D Right)
    (onpeg E Right)
    (onpeg F Right)
    (onpeg G Right)

    ;; clear markers: A is the top disk; Left and Middle are empty (clear).
    (clear A)
    (clear Left)
    (clear Middle)
    ;; Right is not clear because A sits on it (through chain)
    ;; Other disks are not clear (they have disks above them)
    ;; s1 is enabled as the first step if a fully-ordered execution is desired
    (step-enabled s1)
    ;; chain next-step relationships (optional scaffolding to reflect a fully ordered 127-step plan).
    ;; We include the full chain s1 -> s2 -> ... -> s128 so a planner that chooses to use planned-move facts
    ;; can enforce precise ordering. These facts are optional: a planner can solve purely by dynamics
    ;; or use the planned-move scaffolding if it wants to force the exact sequence below.
    (next-step s1 s2) (next-step s2 s3) (next-step s3 s4) (next-step s4 s5) (next-step s5 s6)
    (next-step s6 s7) (next-step s7 s8) (next-step s8 s9) (next-step s9 s10) (next-step s10 s11)
    (next-step s11 s12) (next-step s12 s13) (next-step s13 s14) (next-step s14 s15) (next-step s15 s16)
    (next-step s16 s17) (next-step s17 s18) (next-step s18 s19) (next-step s19 s20) (next-step s20 s21)
    (next-step s21 s22) (next-step s22 s23) (next-step s23 s24) (next-step s24 s25) (next-step s25 s26)
    (next-step s26 s27) (next-step s27 s28) (next-step s28 s29) (next-step s29 s30) (next-step s30 s31)
    (next-step s31 s32) (next-step s32 s33) (next-step s33 s34) (next-step s34 s35) (next-step s35 s36)
    (next-step s36 s37) (next-step s37 s38) (next-step s38 s39) (next-step s39 s40) (next-step s40 s41)
    (next-step s41 s42) (next-step s42 s43) (next-step s43 s44) (next-step s44 s45) (next-step s45 s46)
    (next-step s46 s47) (next-step s47 s48) (next-step s48 s49) (next-step s49 s50) (next-step s50 s51)

    "pddl_domain": "(define (domain hanoi-multiagent)\n  ;; Tower of Hanoi domain for FastDownward-compatible STRIPS planning\n  ;; Types:\n  ;;  - place: an abstract type for supports (pegs and disks)\n  ;;  - peg  and disk are subtypes of place\n  (:requirements :strips :typing :negative-preconditions)\n  (:types place peg disk)\n\n  ;; Predicates:\n  ;; (on ?d ?s)         : disk ?d is directly on support ?s (support = peg or disk)\n  ;; (onpeg ?d ?p)      : disk ?d is located on base peg ?p (the peg under its stack)\n  ;; (clear ?s)         : support ?s (peg or disk) has nothing on top (i.e., it is top)\n  ;; (smaller ?d1 ?d2)  : disk ?d1 is strictly smaller than disk ?d2\n  ;; The planning instance will provide the concrete initial facts for these predicates.\n  (:predicates\n    (on ?d - disk ?s - place)\n    (onpeg ?d - disk ?p - peg)\n    (clear ?s - place)\n    (smaller ?d1 - disk ?d2 - disk)\n    ;; The next predicates are used if a planner trace-enforcing ordering is required.\n    ;; They are included to allow expressing explicit ordered-step constraints in the problem.\n    (step-done ?st)\n    (step-enabled ?st)\n    (planned-move ?st ?d - disk ?src - peg ?dst - peg)\n    (next-step ?st1 ?st2)\n  )\n\n  ;; Single primitive action: move the top disk associated with a source peg to a destination peg.\n  ;; The action is guarded so it can only move a disk when:\n  ;;  - the disk is currently the top item of its source peg (onpeg ?d ?src and clear ?d)\n  ;;  - the destination peg's top (if any) is larger than the moving disk, or the destination peg is empty (clear ?dst)\n  ;; To support both placing onto an empty peg and onto another disk, the action requires the current\n  ;; immediate support of the moved disk (?support) and, when placing onto a disk, the target top disk (?target-top).\n  ;; Note: We keep one action schema that supports both cases by requiring the caller/environment ensure\n  ;; the appropriate clear/size facts for the destination.\n  (:action move-top\n    :parameters (?st ?next - (either ?step ?step)\n                ?d - disk\n                ?support - place\n                ?src - peg\n                ?dst - peg\n                ?target-top - disk)\n    :precondition (and\n      ;; sequencing guard: if the problem includes planned-move facts and step enabling, require step-enabled\n      (or (not (planned-move ?st ?d ?src ?dst)) (step-enabled ?st))\n      ;; the disk is directly on its immediate support\n      (on ?d ?support)\n      ;; the disk is reported as associated to source peg\n      (onpeg ?d ?src)\n      ;; the disk is top of whatever it's on (no disk above)\n      (clear ?d)\n      ;; destination is either empty (no disk on top of the peg) OR has a top disk ?target-top which is clear and larger\n      ;; We express this by requiring either (clear ?dst) or (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (clear ?target-top) (smaller ?d ?target-top))\n      ;; Because STRIPS does not have direct OR, callers must ensure one of these holds in the initial state evolution.\n      ;; We'll test both forms at runtime through the available predicates.\n      ;; For safety we require that either the destination peg is clear OR the indicated top disk exists and is larger.\n      ;; (The planner must ensure one of these is true for the action to be applicable.)\n      (or (clear ?dst) (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (clear ?target-top) (smaller ?d ?target-top)))\n    )\n    :effect (and\n      ;; sequencing effects: mark this step done and enable successor step if planning a fully-ordered execution\n      (when (planned-move ?st ?d ?src ?dst)\n        (and (not (step-enabled ?st)) (step-done ?st) (step-enabled ?next)))\n      ;; update structural relations for the moved disk: remove its old on fact and set its new direct support\n      (not (on ?d ?support))\n      ;; When placing on empty peg, direct support becomes the dst peg; when placing on top of another disk, new support becomes that disk.\n      ;; Because the action includes ?target-top param, we cover both cases:\n      ;; If destination was empty, the new direct support is the destination peg (we add on ?d ?dst).\n      ;; If destination had a top disk ?target-top, the new direct support is that disk (we add on ?d ?target-top).\n      (or\n        (and (clear ?dst) (on ?d ?dst))\n        (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (not (clear ?target-top)) (on ?d ?target-top))\n      )\n      ;; update onpeg (base peg) mapping: the moved disk is now associated with destination peg\n      (not (onpeg ?d ?src))\n      (onpeg ?d ?dst)\n      ;; update clear flags:\n      ;; the moved disk remains clear (it is top on its new support)\n      ;; the previous support becomes clear (since d was top on it and moved)\n      (clear ?support)\n      ;; the destination support (peg or disk) is no longer clear after placing d on it\n      (not (clear ?dst))\n      (when (and (on ?target-top ?dst) (clear ?target-top))\n        (not (clear ?target-top)))\n    )\n  )\n)",
    "pddl_problem": "(define (problem hanoi-7-disks)\n  (:domain hanoi-multiagent)\n\n  ;; Objects: 7 disks A..G and three pegs Left, Middle, Right.\n  (:objects\n    A B C D E F G - disk\n    Left Middle Right - peg\n    ;;
